 717 # bug #4103220 should be adequately tested by the above tests, which represent a pretty
 718 # good cross-section of the locale data
 719 
 720 # bug #4103861
 721 # As far as I can tell, French dates do not use commas at all.  However, we
 722 # already have a comma after the month in the LONG date format, so we want to be
 723 # consistent with that.  This is probably taken from the Windows locale data,
 724 # which does include a comma after month for fr_CA (although not for fr_FR).
 725 # Hence: No comma after the day of week. ASL 5/12/98
 726 # Follow-up: Well, a follow-up duplicate bug (4141637) has confirmed that the
 727 # comma should not be present at all in French.  Removing the comma.
 728 FormatData/fr_CA/DatePatterns/0=EEEE d MMMM y
 729 FormatData/fr_CA/DatePatterns/1=d MMMM y
 730 FormatData/en_CA/DatePatterns/0=EEEE, MMMM d, y
 731

 719 
 720 # bug #4103861
 721 # As far as I can tell, French dates do not use commas at all.  However, we
 722 # already have a comma after the month in the LONG date format, so we want to be
 723 # consistent with that.  This is probably taken from the Windows locale data,
 724 # which does include a comma after month for fr_CA (although not for fr_FR).
 725 # Hence: No comma after the day of week. ASL 5/12/98
 726 # Follow-up: Well, a follow-up duplicate bug (4141637) has confirmed that the
 727 # comma should not be present at all in French.  Removing the comma.
 728 FormatData/fr_CA/DatePatterns/0=EEEE d MMMM y
 729 FormatData/fr_CA/DatePatterns/1=d MMMM y
 730 FormatData/en_CA/DatePatterns/0=EEEE, MMMM d, y
